				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Die Elenden sollen essen, BWV 75 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>14 movements (2 parts)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1723
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>Bach's first Cantata as Thomaskantor.
</p>
<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Commentary_on_the_movements">Commentary on the movements</span></h4>
<p><b>Prima parte</b>
</p>
<ol><li>Chorus: Die Elenden sollen essen. A slow-fast French Overture-like movement. 
</li><li>Recitativo (Bass): Was hilft des Purpurs Majestät. Recitative with string accompaniment. 
</li><li>Aria (Tenor): Mein Jesus soll mein alles sein. Aria with strings and oboes. The tenor entry is on a "decidedly vocal 'motto'"<sup>1</sup>. Also, this could perhaps be a polonaise. 
</li><li>Recitativo (Tenor): Gott stürzet und erhöhet. Secco recitative. 
</li><li>Aria (Soprano): Ich nehme mein Leiden. A "minuet"-like aria with obbligato oboe d'amore. 
</li><li>Recitativo (Soprano): Indes schenkt Gott ein gut Gewissen. Secco recitative. 
</li><li>Choral: Was Gott tut, das ist wohlgetan. A more generous chorale setting than usual, with much independent writing. 
</li></ol>
<p><b>Seconda parte</b>
</p>
<ol><li>Sinfonia. A sinfonia for trumpet and strings. However, the composition is really just a chorale arrangement again. 
</li><li>Recitativo (Alto): Nur eines kränkt. Recitative with string accompaniment. 
</li><li>Aria (Alto): Jesus macht mich geistlich reich. A "quasi-passepied"<sup>1</sup>. The obbligato here is unison violins.
</li><li>Recitativo (Bass): Wer nur in Jesu bleibt. Secco recitative. 
</li><li>Aria (Bass): Mein Herze glaubt und liebt. The trumpet here has a juicy concertante part in the final aria. 
</li><li>Recitativo (Tenor): O Armut, der kein Reichtum gleicht! Secco recitative. 
</li><li>Choral: Was Gott tut, das ist wohlgetan. A more generous chorale setting than usual, with much independent writing. 
</li></ol>
<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Print_Sources_Consulted">Print Sources Consulted</span></h4>
<ul><li>Dürr, Alfred. <i><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://astore.amazon.com/intemusiscorl-20/detail/0199297762/">The Cantatas of J.S. Bach</a></span></i>. 2 ed. Richard D.P. Jones (Trans). 
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>Oxford: Oxford University Press, 2005. 
</dd></dl>
